| 1:48:20| I'd like to read it into the record, please.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6500)|
| 1:48:26| Whereas Henry T. Ellenberg was born and raised in Knoxville, educated at Beaumont Elementary School| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6506)|
| 1:48:32| and Rule High School, where his education was interrupted to serve in World War II as a medic| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6512)|
| 1:48:37| with the 217th General Hospital attachment to General Patton's Third Army.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6517)|
| 1:48:42| And whereas Mr. Ellenberg returned to Knoxville to obtain his GED and later attended the University of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6522)|
| 1:48:48| where he received certifications in business, insurance, and real estate.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6528)|
| 1:48:53| And whereas as an entrepreneur, Henry, along with his wife, Fay Freeman Ellenberg,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6533)|
| 1:49:00| raised and educated their three children.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6540)|
| 1:49:04| And whereas Henry owned and operated several businesses, including Wholesale Auto Parts,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6544)|
| 1:49:09| Ellenberg's Radiator Service, and Velda Rose Dry Cleaners.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6549)|
| 1:49:13| And whereas as a member of Central Baptist Church of Fountain City, Mr. Ellenberg taught Sunday school for over 20 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6553)|
| 1:49:21| Whereas always concerned about children, Henry supported sports teams| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6561)|
| 1:49:26| and worked to establish and light Badgett Field.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6566)|
| 1:49:30| And whereas for many years Henry worked tirelessly with Fountain City Lions Club| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6570)|
| 1:49:36| and also served civically in leadership with the West Haven Business and Professional Association.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6576)|
| 1:49:42| And whereas Henry was always interested in helping others help themselves| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6582)|
| 1:49:47| and frequently became their advocate with government.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6587)|
| 1:49:50| And whereas Henry Ellenberg served a term on the Knoxville Housing Authority,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6590)|
| 1:49:54| which later became Knoxville's Community Development Corporation, KCDC.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6594)|
| 1:49:59| And whereas answering the call to further service, Henry was elected to serve| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6599)|
| 1:50:04| as a councilman at large on Knoxville City Council,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6604)|
| 1:50:08| where he served as the chairman of the airport committee and on the Metropolitan Airport Authority.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6608)|
| 1:50:13| And whereas Henry's service on these boards was during the time when the airport runways were extended| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6613)|
| 1:50:19| to their present length to accommodate larger planes, a new terminal was constructed| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6619)|
| 1:50:24| and critical planning for the 1982 World's Fair was undertaken.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6624)|
| 1:50:28| And whereas following his council years, Henry and Judge Howard Bozeman worked tirelessly| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6628)|
| 1:50:34| without remuneration to secure the grants to establish the present Knox County Housing Authority, the KCHA.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6634)|
| 1:50:45| And whereas Henry later served as the KCHA's first full-time executive director overseeing the construction| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6645)|
| 1:50:52| and development of the Virginia Walker and Dutch Town housing developments| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6652)|
| 1:50:56| and the initiation of Section 8 housing for the county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6656)|
| 1:50:59| And whereas always concerned with physically responsible government,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6659)|
| 1:51:03| Henry represented the city of Knoxville and Knox County on numerous bond issues| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6663)|
| 1:51:08| and frequently spoke of his pride of our exemplary bond rating.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6668)|
| 1:51:13| And whereas Henry Ellenberg finished his public service in the state revenue office in Knoxville.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6673)|
| 1:51:19| And whereas Henry's numerous friends and colleagues remember him for his energy,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6679)|
| 1:51:25| his resourcefulness and ability to problem solve, his availability and most of all his affable sense of humor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6685)|
| 1:51:34| Now therefore be it resolved by the commission of Knox County as follows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6694)|
| 1:51:38| The commission of Knox County hereby memorializes Henry T. Ellenberg for his leadership,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6698)|
| 1:51:44| service and sacrifice to Knox County and extends their sincere condolences to his family and friends.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6704)|

| 1:56:33| Whereas Rural Metro Division General Manager Rob Webb was recently honored for his appointment by Governor Phil Bredesen| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=6993)|
| 1:56:40| to the Tennessee Emergency Medical Services Board as a representative for ambulance service operators.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7000)|
| 1:56:45| And whereas the Tennessee Emergency Medical Services Board oversees the Tennessee Emergency Medical Services Division| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7005)|
| 1:56:52| and is responsible for establishing all rules governing statewide emergency systems,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7012)|
| 1:56:57| which is comprised of thousands of paramedics from 210 ambulance service companies operating over 1,300 ambulances| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7017)|
| 1:57:05| and transporting over a million patients annually.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7025)|
| 1:57:10| And whereas the rules and protocols established by the prestigious board help ensure that the same high standard of care| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7030)|
| 1:57:16| is available in Tennessee's rural counties as well as its metro areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocom090824part1?start=7036)|
